At noon, he went to the Central Bank to handle important official business and met with Chen Xing, Vice President of the Central Bank, and Yang Ge, Advisor to the Ministry of Finance, and many others. A reporter from the Central News Agency went to the Central Bank yesterday to inquire about the current situation. According to him, the Central Government has decided to focus on the overall situation and deal with the changes in Guangdong and Guangxi with leniency. It hopes that the troops in Guangdong and Guangxi will immediately withdraw to their original defenses and hopes that comrades in Guangdong and Guangxi will come to Beijing to attend the Second Plenary Session. If there are any opinions, they can be discussed, and everything can be resolved. According to news I have obtained, Chen Bonan has telegraphed his troops to stop advancing and will send a responsible representative to Beijing to pay respects to and consult with the Central Authorities. As for the report that the Central Government will send personnel to the south, I am busy with my duties and have no intention of going to the south at present. I have not heard of the rumors that Ye Chucang, Wang Chonghui, and others will go to the south. He then talked about the source of smuggled goods, which should be prevented and cracked down on. The sales channels of smuggled goods are also very important. He hoped that merchants and people across the country would uphold their patriotic enthusiasm and investigate the source of goods they buy. If they are smuggled goods, they should not buy them. If smuggled goods have no sales market, those who operate smuggled goods will naturally disappear. Moreover, the government has regulations for those who report smuggled goods, and they will be rewarded with 50%. In this way, our patriotic merchants and people can express their patriotic hearts and also benefit from a 50% bonus. The society may not know about this, and I hope the newspapers will publicize it so that everyone knows about it. With the cooperation of the government and the people, the smuggling problem can be fundamentally resolved.

Beijing-Shanghai Railway Purchase of Vehicle Advances Fully Repaid 92

The Ministry of Railways Notifies the Sino-British Bank to Cancel the Vehicle Purchase Advance Contract

Shin Shi News Agency said that the Beijing-Shanghai Railway signed a vehicle purchase advance contract with the Sino-British Bank in June of the 18th year of the Republic of China. Interest was charged at 8% per week from the date of payment for the purchase of materials, totaling 161,574 pounds, 13 shillings, and 2 pence. Since the Ministry of Railways supervised the two railway bureaus to deposit special reserve funds from the business revenue to repay the debts on a monthly basis and allocated them to the HSBC Bank to transfer to the Sino-British Bank in London for repayment, the advance payment has been fully repaid as of recently. Now the Railway Bureau has submitted a request to the Ministry of Railways to notify the Sino-British Bank to cancel the advance payment contract.

Completion of the Yue-Han Railway 6% British Boxer Indemnity Bond Management Committee Ends 93

The Zhushao section of the project is completed and the bond funds have been fully disbursed.

Shin Shi News Agency said that in order to complete the Yue-Han Railway, the Ministry of Railways, together with the Ministry of Finance, issued the 6% British Boxer Indemnity Bond in the 23rd year of the Republic of China. According to the regulations of the bond, a Bond Management Committee should be established. The three ministries of Railways, Finance and Audit, and the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Board of Directors mutually sent representatives to organize and establish the committee to handle the management and disbursement of the bond funds. It has been nearly two years since then, and a total of 1.35 million pounds of bond funds have been received successively, which have been allocated for the construction of the Zhushao section of the Yue-Han Railway. Now the construction project of the Zhushao section has been largely completed, and it has been decided to officially open to traffic on September 1. The bond funds managed by the committee have also been fully disbursed one after another. According to Article 8 of the committee's organizational regulations, "It shall be abolished on the date when the bond funds are fully disbursed," it should be announced immediately. The committee has followed the regulations to handle the liquidation and reported to the Ministry of Finance. The Ministry of Finance has also designated the receiving agencies and taken over all documents, archives, official seals, account books, etc.

Completing the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway, Issuing 6% English Gold Bonds 95

A Total of One Million and One Hundred Thousand Pounds Sterling at 6% Annual Interest, Underwritten by Bank of China, Bank of Communications, and HSBC

In order to complete the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway, the Ministry of Railways submitted a proposal to the Executive Yuan and the Legislative Yuan for approval and signed a loan contract with a consortium formed by the British Chinese Corporation and the China Construction Bank on May 8th of this year. The loan amounts to one million and one hundred thousand pounds sterling, and bonds are issued, underwritten by the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, and HSBC. A fund custody committee is established. The details are as follows:

Issuing Bonds: The total amount of bonds is one million and one hundred thousand pounds sterling. The repayment period is from 1941 to 1960. The bonds are underwritten by the Central Bank, the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, and HSBC at a rate of 94, that is, each bond with a face value of one hundred pounds sterling will actually receive ninety-four pounds sterling. The interest rate is six percent per annum, with principal and interest repaid on June 15th and December 15th each year. The first interest payment will be made on December 15th of this year. Holders of the loan's principal and interest who are paid in Shanghai may request the exchange rate for immediate English gold drafts payable in London, in exchange for Chinese legal tender. The bonds are divided into two types: fifty pounds and one hundred pounds.

Use and Guarantee: In order to repay the remaining balance of the 1908 Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway loan and to meet the funding needs for the uncompleted sections of the railway, the Ministry of Railways signed a contract with the above-mentioned consortium on November 29th of the 23rd year of the Republic of China to raise a loan of sixteen million yuan in national currency. However, due to financial and market conditions at the time, the funds were not raised. The consortium advanced funds twice on behalf of the Ministry of Railways in May of the 24th year of the Republic of China, one to repay the remaining balance of the above-mentioned 1908 loan, and the other to provide funds for the commencement of the Qiantang River Bridge. Now, in order to complete the original loan plan of the 23rd year of the Republic of China, a new contract for this loan of one million and one hundred thousand pounds sterling was re-signed on May 8th of the 25th year of the Republic of China, directly by the National Government, and the income of the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway (including 70% of the toll revenue from the railway and highway traffic on the Qiantang River Bridge, with the remaining 30% belonging to the Zhejiang Provincial Government) was designated as the first guarantee, and the funds that can be designated by the Ministry of Railways as the second guarantee. The above-mentioned income of the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway has not been pledged for any loan and can be used exclusively for the repayment of the principal and interest of this loan. The loan is used exclusively for (1) repaying the above-mentioned two advances, (2) repaying the outstanding payments owed to the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Railway Company since the 3rd year of the Republic of China, (3) completing the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway and the Qiantang River Bridge, (4) constructing the Nanxingqiao branch line, and (5) paying for the price of vehicles ordered through the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Board of Trustees. The term is 25 years, starting from the 29th year of the Republic of China, with principal repaid by lottery. Each lottery shall be held in Shanghai three months before each repayment. However, the National Government may, at any time, according to the following methods, notify the consortium in writing six months in advance to repay in advance. From ten years after the loan is established to the sixteenth year, the bonds will be redeemed at face value plus 2.5% (that is, each bond with a face value of one hundred pounds sterling will be redeemed at one hundred and two pounds and ten shillings sterling). After the sixteenth year, the bonds may be redeemed at the face value of the bonds.

Four Banks Underwrite: The underwriting methods of the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, and HSBC are (1) Application: Applicants should fill out an application form, and the application amount should be in units of fifty pounds sterling. (2) Payment: The amount to be raised should be paid in full once by London telegraphic transfer (telegraphic fees are borne by the bank). (3) Refund: If the amount raised is insufficient to allocate the excess, the bank will refund all or part of the bond funds that have been paid. (4) Subscription Certificate: Applicants should exchange the bond notification for an unregistered subscription certificate from the bank. When the bonds are ready, the prospectus, recruitment prospectus, and application form can be obtained from the above-mentioned banks, or from the British Chinese Corporation at 27 Bund, Shanghai, and the China Construction Bank at 181 Jiangxi Road. (6) Application Forms: Registration has already begun and will be closed on or before June 17th. After the recruitment registration began, the number of people going to the four underwriting banks and the two British-Chinese Construction Banks to obtain stamps and application forms was very enthusiastic yesterday. As soon as the full amount is reached, the registration will be closed immediately. The majority of applicants are British people residing in Shanghai.

Fund Committee: The Custody Fund Committee. The Ministry of Railways appointed five committee members. In addition to Minister Zhang Gongquan, who served as a committee member and chairman, Song Ziliang, general manager of the China Construction Bank, Davidson, the resident representative of the British Chinese Corporation in Shanghai, represented the consortium, and Sa Fuzun and Lin Zhaotang represented the Ministry of Railways, with full supervisory powers. In addition, foreign committee members were invited to participate in the joint management system implemented by the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways, and the employment of a British Chief Accountant and a British Chief Engineer was maintained. The railway income is deposited monthly in the HSBC and the Bank of China as a fund for repaying the principal and interest in English gold. The British Chinese Corporation and the China Construction Bank have been appointed as the special agents for the bondholders. If there is a surplus in the railway income, it should be deposited in the bank as a special deposit. The amount of this deposit should be sufficient to cover the principal and interest payable on this loan for two years. According to the statistics published by the railway, the average annual net profit of the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway in the past five years was 1,518,551 yuan and 8551 yuan in national currency. In particular, the net profit in the 20th year of the Republic of China reached a record high of 2 million yuan in national currency. Although the situation in the 23rd and 24th years of the Republic of China was slightly worse, the net profit still reached 1,344,928 yuan in national currency. Therefore, after the establishment of this loan, the annual interest payment for the first five years, calculated at an exchange rate of one shilling, two pence, and three-eighths, is 1,100,1913 yuan and 03 yuan in national currency. There is still a sufficient surplus in annual income that can be used as a special deposit. It is expected that after the completion of the section from Zhakou to Baiguan (including the Qiantang River Bridge), the operating income should increase significantly. On the one hand, the Fund Management Committee of this loan, for the benefit of protecting bondholders, shall exercise its supervisory powers and assist the railway operation in terms of economy and savings in expenses as much as possible. After the completion of the railway, the annual income can be increased by at least 720,000 yuan in national currency. In addition, it is estimated that the Qiantang River Bridge will generate 300,000 yuan in national currency per year, for a total increase of 1,020,000 yuan in national currency per year. The consortium also intends to apply to the London Stock Exchange for permission to officially open the bonds of this loan on the Exchange to facilitate circulation. If members of the Shanghai Stock Exchange apply for subscriptions, they should be given 2.5 per thousand of the amount of bonds allocated as commission.

Notify Villagers: If smuggled goods are discovered, they should be reported to the Customs or local military police for investigation and arrest at any time. After the smuggled goods are seized, the Customs will deal with them strictly and reward them generously in accordance with the regulations to encourage them. At this time of turmoil and shared destiny, we sincerely hope that you will assist us sincerely and work together to overcome difficulties. We look forward to receiving your telegrams. "We have endless things to say," etc. Upon receipt of this, we found that customs duties are a major source of national revenue and are extremely important. The current smuggling situation is serious, and administrative agencies in various places should at any time

Assist in Investigation and Arrest: In order to maintain national taxes, the reason for the previous telegram was, "In addition to separately ordering the Chief Administrative Inspectors of each district to follow the instructions and supervise their subordinates, it is necessary to assist in the handling carefully," etc. Upon receipt of this, it is hereby ordered that the county magistrate assist in the investigation and arrest at any time.

A Large Number of Locomotive Engines from the Pinghan Railway are Shipped to Shanghai for Repair 96

It Will Take Two Years to Complete the Repairs

Regarding the Pinghan Railway, there are approximately fifty locomotive engines that have been damaged over the years and cannot be used, and many locomotives must have all parts disassembled for major repairs. It is now learned that the authorities of the railway have decided to ship the locomotives to Shanghai for repair because the Wusong Railway Factory of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway is well-equipped and has a very rich supply of materials. A contract has now been negotiated. It is also learned that recently, seven Pinghan locomotives that were shipped to the factory have begun to be dismantled and construction has begun ahead of schedule. It is estimated that the project will take about two years to complete all repairs.

The Xiang Embankment in Hubei Collapses, a Post-Disaster Engineering Committee is Organized 98

The Breach in the Xiang Embankment is Approximately 500 Meters, and Completion Can Be Rushed in About 20 Days

The collapse of the Xiang Embankment in Hubei Province is of great importance to the entire embankment project in the province. Kong Xiangxi, Standing Committee Member of the National Economic Council and Chairman of the Water Conservancy Committee, specially appointed Qin Fen, Secretary-General of the Council, to fly to Wuhan on the 7th of this month to inspect the construction site and to plan remedial measures in order to seal the breach as soon as possible. It is now learned that Secretary-General Qin has returned to Beijing today, and proper measures have been determined for the post-disaster engineering of the Xiang Embankment, and a post-disaster engineering committee has been organized, with Fan Shaogai as the chairman. The committee will be fully responsible for the planning and management of the project based on the measures agreed upon by the Economic Council and the Hubei Provincial Government, in order to expedite the process. It is reported that the breach is approximately 500 meters, and the rest is still intact. If the weather is clear, it is expected that completion can be rushed in about 20 days. It is also reported that the Post-Disaster Engineering Committee of the Xiang Embankment was organized on the 11th of this month, and is now supervising employees to work day and night in order to seal the breach as soon as possible.

Various Countries Initiate Celebrations for Yu Qiaqing's 70th Birthday 104

Central News Agency: Yu Qiaqing is enthusiastic about public welfare and charity, and has made many contributions to the Party and the country over the years. July 6th of this year marks his 70th birthday and the 55th anniversary of his residence in Shanghai. Mayor Wu and leaders from all sectors have initiated a move to transfer birthday gifts for the construction of the Yu Qiaqing Anti-Tuberculosis Hospital, and have designated the coastal area of Wusong as the site for the hospital. It has also been decided to develop it into a park for commemoration. Recently, representatives from all sectors convened a meeting and appointed Du Yuesheng, Wang Xiaolai, Yu Zuoting, Li Tingan, Li Dachao, and others as members of the preparatory committee for the Yu Qiaqing Anti-Tuberculosis Hospital. The office is located in the Ningbo Fellow Countrymen Association. A commemorative meeting will be held at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce on July 4th, inviting participation from all sectors. Mayor Wu will also invite foreign dignitaries to attend. On the 5th and 6th, celebrations will be held at the Ningbo Fellow Countrymen Association. Invitations have been sent to various organizations and leaders from all sectors, requesting their enthusiastic support to jointly accomplish this great undertaking. The origin of the project is recorded below:

(Solicitation for Essays on Mr. Yu Qiaqing's 70th Birthday and 55th Anniversary in Shanghai, and the Establishment of the Yu Qiaqing Anti-Tuberculosis Hospital in Wusong) It is said, "To let those who know first awaken those who know later, to let those who are aware first awaken those who are aware later." "Knowing" and "being aware" are listed equally, but the meaning is vastly different. Knowing is a matter of acquired knowledge, while being aware is a matter of innate ability. Knowing comes from accumulation and gradual development, while being aware arises suddenly from nothing. Is Mr. Yu Qiaqing of Zhenhai a man of foreknowledge or a man of foresight? Please examine his life and deeds to judge for yourselves. Mr. Yu came to Shanghai at the age of fifteen to study commerce. Upon entering the market, his talent astonished the experienced merchants. Within a few years, he went from being an employee of the Ruikang Dye Company to a compradore of the Lu Lin Foreign Firm. At a young age, he dominated the market and presided over public associations, which was rare since the opening of the port. Commercial affairs emphasize the accumulation of capital rather than rapid progress, and rely on experience rather than sudden changes. Mr. Yu broke the ordinary commercial history, like a dragon appearing in the fields. In the past, it was rare to see such a change. Who else but Mr. Yu, endowed with creative commercial talent, could have achieved this? Moreover, Mr. Yu is a businessman who excels in business, and his ambition is like an affair. He transforms to engage in politics, and politics is guided by Mr. Yu's ambition. He is not like an official who only works in one position and only serves one region. I once commented that since the opening of Shanghai, the Manchu government has been ignorant of foreign affairs. They signed treaties that ceded rights and humiliated the country without end. The people who were born, raised, and made their living here were restricted and bound by these treaties. They were not allowed to complain or seek redress. They had almost accepted this as their second nature, content to remain in this state forever. But Mr. Yu was like a morning rooster in Runan, mounting the platform to awaken the people. After a long period of accumulation, he took advantage of the dawn to fight for clarity. A great wave was formed, overturning the foreign powers, starting with the cemetery case and followed by the uproar in the public hall. What was the cemetery case? The Siming Public Cemetery was a public area established by the people of Ningbo to honor their ancestors. The people of Ningbo value friendship and righteousness above all else, and they cherish their ancestral graves even more. Thus, the French attempted to seize the land, but they were repeatedly thwarted. Mr. Yu, along with Yan Xiaofang, Ye Chengzhong, Shen Zhongli, and other elders, took charge of the matter and refused to yield. Therefore, on May 28th of the 24th year of Guangxu, the French Consul Bai Zhaotai, realizing that empty threats would not work, hastily mobilized troops to destroy the cemetery walls, determined to seize the public cemetery. The situation suddenly became dire. Yan, Ye, Shen, and others were at a loss. Mr. Yu said, "The French destroy the cemetery walls because the cemetery has no country to protect it. They destroy the country because the country has no people to choose it. If the cemetery walls are destroyed, the country is destroyed. If the country is destroyed, the people are destroyed. We must stand up for the people and fight for the country. People must stand up for the country and fight for the cemetery walls." His thoughts circled like a ring, unspoken but like an order. Next, he used the people of Ningbo to represent the people of the country, and used himself to represent the people of Ningbo's deep awareness, like a shadow following its form, almost without thinking, and so it was. Mr. Yu was furious, and all the people of Shanghai gathered at his command. The case started with Shen Hongmai raising objections, and ended with Bai Zhaotai apologizing. Mr. Yu commanded with calm assurance, as if nothing had happened. His achievement was as great as Xiang Ru's saving Zhao's walls, and his plan was superior to the Lu people's returning the invaded land. This was the most important battle, in which he used righteousness to manage affairs and made decisive decisions. Without precedent or external support, who can say from what source this awareness came? Seven years later, a Cantonese woman named Huang, whose husband had died in Sichuan, was taking her maid back to Guangdong via Shanghai. The Municipal Council accused her of trafficking in persons and detained her. Councilor Jin Gongbo argued for her release. The Western police made a great disturbance, and the so-called New Yamen was instructed by the British Vice Consul De Wei to have the police beat Jin at the gate, tearing his official robes. The people heard this and went on strike. The Western merchants also went on strike in response. The situation was very precarious. At that time, the Manchu Prince Zai Ze was passing through Shanghai on his way to study constitutional government abroad. Yuan Shuxun, the Customs Taotai, was also helpless. Mr. Yu then invited Zhu Baosan, Zhou Jinzhen, Shi Ziying, and others to mediate. After repeated efforts, they finally reached a settlement. De Wei was dismissed, the police chief was punished, and more than 500 arrested people were released. The cloudy sky cleared. Our country had long been restricted by the consular jurisdiction system. At this point, we showed the true strength of the people and took a step toward recovering legal rights. People praised Mr. Yu's ability to plan carefully and never give up when facing difficulties. Who gave Mr. Yu this awareness? Was it Dong Zhongshu's effort to understand or Lao Tzu's natural transformation? After this, foreigners began to respect us. How did we achieve self-governance? Mr. Yu's first priority was to establish himself and others. He resisted the powerful forces from the outside and upheld righteousness from the inside. The Chinese seat on the Municipal Council was available, but it was limited to Mr. Yu alone. Mr. Yu said this was an insult to the Chinese people. Then he invited Hu Jimei and Yuan Hengzhi to build a sports field in Zhabei, change to yellow uniforms, and undergo training to advocate for this. Many merchants joined Mr. Yu. The Chinese self-defense force became a reality. The Chinese team in the International Chamber of Commerce was formed. This team was effective in resisting foreign aggression and protecting merchants. The idea of revolution at the end of the Qing Dynasty was also fostered because of this. During the Xinhai Revolution, Mr. Yu and Mr. Chen Qimei relied on this force to restore Shanghai and Songhu. Later, the southern provinces followed suit. Governor Cheng Dequan of Suzhou was able to revolt because of Mr. Yu's mediation and assistance. The republic was founded, and the north and south were united. Everyone thought they had made a great contribution and celebrated, but Mr. Yu did not participate. For more than ten years, the political system changed, but democracy did not advance. Young people were angry and could not be restrained. In May of the 14th year, Shanghai students demonstrated against the Northern government. The Western police fired 44 shots and injured people, causing great disorder. The turmoil was no less than the previous cemetery case and the uproar in the public hall. How did he manage to suppress and coordinate to restore peace, so that the people commemorate the May 30th Incident to this day, without losing the great significance of the national rights movement in history? All of this was due to Mr. Yu's handling of the matter at that time. Everyone says that Fan Zhongyan was the first to worry about the world and the last to enjoy it. Mr. Yu believes that there has never been joy in the world. His own worries have no order. How great is Mr. Yu! The drowned are drowning, the hungry are hungry. For 55 years, he has served the people tirelessly. This is Mr. Yu's heart, but compared to Yu's three passes, eight years is still too short, and his achievements have far exceeded them. At the turn of the Guangxu era, the Chinese first heard about industrial innovation, but they could not implement it. Only Mr. Yu established the Siming Bank and the Ningbo-Shaoxing Steamship Company. The former was to intercept foreign merchants' manipulation of finance, and the latter was to seize foreign ships' monopoly of shipping. The Nanjing Promotion of Righteousness Association was the seed of the national product exhibition. Mr. Yu and Governor-General Duanfang of Jiangsu presided over it. Although the start of this meeting was simple, it will be a great and important event in our industrial history. The hardships and complexities were all managed by Mr. Yu. He forgot his toil and grievances, as if nothing had happened. These are just the most obvious of Mr. Yu's undertakings. These emerging industries in the past 50 years would not have been possible without Mr. Yu's words and actions. Even if his words and actions did not necessarily lead to his involvement, others could succeed. Mr. Yu's principle of action is like this. Moreover, Mr. Yu's awareness is the earliest and most genuine, like water pouring into the ground, penetrating everything. Therefore, he can handle everything calmly and impartially. Recently, he has been taking care of the affairs of the Sanbei Shipping Company and the Longshan Wharf, which are all matters of his hometown. This is a return to simplicity after splendor, to establish a diligent intention and to show his respect for his hometown. It seems that it is not yet time to enjoy the happiness. This year, July 6th marks Mr. Yu's 70th birthday and the 55th anniversary of his residence in Shanghai. We thought we should celebrate it to promote national heroes and wish him longevity. Mr. Yu said no, the country is in such a difficult situation, how can we talk about longevity and commemoration? We said yes, because of the national crisis, Mr. Yu's birthday cannot but be celebrated, and Mr. Yu's deeds cannot but be commemorated. Why? Because if everyone can have Mr. Yu's awareness, or receive his awareness, the country will have no difficulties. Therefore, we all agree with this intention. We will write it down to inspire scholars and allow them to base their own views and celebrate this great man of the world to celebrate the world. We will commemorate this great man of the world to inspire the world. How to celebrate, how to inspire? We all say that anti-tuberculosis is an important health policy today. We should gather funds to build an anti-tuberculosis hospital in Wusong and name it after Mr. Yu to show that we will not forget him. Mr. Yu's kindness will be endless, and the symbol of enlightenment will become clearer with the passage of time. This is the solicitation.

Handling of Ship Collisions by the Maritime Affairs Bureau Transferred to the Ministry for Explanation 105

It is a Mediation and Not an Administrative Punishment, and a Party Who is Dissatisfied Can File a Lawsuit in the Judiciary

The Shanghai Maritime Affairs Bureau previously received a letter from the Supervisory Audit Office inquiring about the nature of the Bureau's Collision Committee. After receiving the letter, the Bureau requested the Ministry of Communications to provide an explanation. Yesterday, it received Instruction No. 5807 from the Ministry of Communications, stating: The report has been noted. The organization of the Ship Collision Dispute Resolution Committee is for mediation purposes. The handling letter clarifying responsibility is not an administrative punishment. It is different from the case where people are dissatisfied with the punishment of the administrative authorities and can file an appeal according to the provisions of the Law on Appeals. If one party is dissatisfied with the handling, they should file a lawsuit directly with the judicial authorities. You should be informed of this order.

Request for Transfer of Jurisdiction - Xu Wancheng's Testimony in Court 108

Initially Unresponsive, He Answered Only After Counsel's Guidance; Judge Refused Bail and Ordered Continued Detention

Xu Wancheng, an editor at the Longwen Bookstore at the intersection of Zhonghua Road and Baiyang Lane in Dananmen, published an advertisement in the Minbao newspaper on June 3rd for a special issue of his work report, "Xu Wancheng's Work Report," promoting his upcoming book. A section in this special issue, entitled "An Investigation into the Dark Side of Chinese Justice," contained

many attacks on the entire Shanghai District Court and implicated Judge Zhao. District Court Judges Zhao Yongzhou and Zhao Yuesheng, citing the mention of Judge Zhao, argued that he should be directed to file charges and that it was discovered Xu Wancheng had previously lost a debt case before Judge Zhao. Furthermore, he had been fined four yuan by the court for failing to affix stamp duty, and upon his failure to pay, the execution division dispatched a bailiff to arrest and detain him. They claimed that these were all private grievances used to libel through newspaper advertisements. Therefore, Judge Zhao and others filed a complaint. Prosecutor Tang Ruxiu of the Prosecutor's Office summoned Xu for questioning, and Xu claimed that Judge Zhao and others had taken bribes, which he had reprinted from other newspapers. The prosecutor was asked to produce the newspapers as evidence. Xu was not detained that day, nor was bail set. Subsequently, on

June 5th, Xu sent a letter to the "Legal Commentary" column of the Minbao newspaper, stating that court clerks openly soliciting money was a fact and that the court's pursuit of libel charges was a face-saving measure, further expressing indignation over the alleged humiliation. Therefore, at 2:00 PM on the 7th of this month, Prosecutor Tang continued the interrogation. However, Xu claimed it was the affair of Du Jiasheng and Tan Zhuohong, etc. The prosecutor pointed out that Du and Tan not only had different characters but also different pronunciations from Zhao, and considered this conduct reprehensible. Xu was immediately detained on charges of obstructing official duties and libel and prosecuted. At 9:30 AM yesterday, Judge Lu Hongyi of the Criminal Division opened the 12th courtroom for trial. Xu Wancheng's attorneys, Shu Shengmin and Ding Zhemin, from his native place, appeared in court. Before Xu was brought into the courtroom, the judge informed the defense attorneys that Xu Wancheng had submitted a petition to the court yesterday requesting a transfer of jurisdiction. Therefore, the case should await the decision of the High Court, and no debate would be held today. At this point, Xu was brought into the courtroom. The judge asked Xu his age, hometown, address, and occupation. Xu replied that he was 31 years old, from Jinshan, Songjiang, and worked as a teacher and editor, residing at the Longwen Bookstore. The judge asked, "Did you publish the work report in the Minbao on June 3rd?" Xu replied, "I am now requesting a transfer of jurisdiction." The judge said, "The transfer of jurisdiction is a matter of transfer; we will question you today first, and you must answer." Xu replied, "I published it. Why did you publish it?" "I want to transfer jurisdiction; this place

cannot question me." The judge said, "The transfer of jurisdiction is a matter for the High Court, and the facts of this case must still be questioned today." "I am requesting a transfer of jurisdiction; I cannot speak," and he pulled out a law book and recited a section of the Criminal Procedure Law on the transfer of jurisdiction. Everyone in the courtroom listening was

speechless. Later, after his defense attorneys guided him, saying that providing testimony was separate from the transfer, and there was no conflict, Xu finally agreed to answer. At this point, the judge continued to question Xu Wancheng: "You published in the newspaper, saying things about a pistol and Judge Zhao and others taking bribes, and so on. What did you mean?" "The stolen pistol was a fact, and writing about the responsibility of the president and others was an emotional outburst from us scholars, so we wrote out the facts." "Do you know you committed a crime?" "I wrote it out; I didn't know it was against the law." "You said court clerks often openly solicit money." "I have witnesses because a court clerk solicited money from me." "What's his name?" "He wouldn't say." "According to what you said, it was one court clerk. Why did you say 'often openly solicit money'?" "When I say 'often,' it could be three people, or one person; it's a matter of sentiment." "What is the name of your witness?" "Liu Lianyuan." "You said Judge Zhao took bribes; which Judge Zhao?" "I saw an image in the newspaper of a judge being escorted to Nanjing. Later, flipping through old newspapers, I learned it was Du Jiasheng. I remembered wrongly, mistaking him for Zhao Jiasheng; it was a case from Pudong." "Du Jiasheng is a prosecutor, not a judge. Judge Tan Zhuohong also committed a crime and was escorted to Suzhou. It was this mistake." "The Minbao of June 5th was also sent and published in your name, saying that court clerks solicit money is real, and that the court is suing you for libel in the matter of Judge Zhao as a face-saving measure?" "It was an error about Du and Tan." At this point in the interrogation, the judge announced

suspension of the trial to await submission to higher authorities and review after the ruling on the transfer of jurisdiction. The defendant's attorney immediately requested bail in court. The judge said that after he published in the newspaper on the 3rd of this month, the prosecutor summoned him to court but did not grant bail. Yet he published again, insulting the court. In his mind, there is simply no court or law. Therefore, bail is denied. Xu Wancheng, anxious, said, "My attorney can guarantee it; I won't publish in the newspaper again." The judge said, "You will still await the ruling of the High Court." Xu then said, "I am sick." The judge said, "If you are sick, there is a medical officer in the detention center. If you are severely ill, you can be sent to the Xinpu Yutang. Bail is still denied." He then ordered Judicial Police Chief Zhang Shuping and others to take him down and return him to custody.

Court Approves Suspension of Jiang Xingjie Estate Case 109

Both Parties Reached Agreement on Principles Outside of Court - Establishing an Estate Clearing Committee

After the death of Nanjing-based Shanghai tycoon Jiang Xingjie, his youngest son, Jiang Guopei, claimed that all the estate was controlled by his stepmother, Jiang Yang, and his elder brothers, Guo You and Guo Zhang. He hired attorneys He Shiming and Fan Gang to file a property division lawsuit with the First Special District Court, demanding one-third of his late father's estate of three million yuan, totaling one million yuan, and requesting a preliminary injunction. The First Special Court had summoned the parties several times. The defendant Jiang Yang's attorneys, Jiang Yiping and Wang Fuchang, stated that the plaintiffs and defendants were mother and sons, brothers, and that reconciliation was preferable. Therefore, the court granted a postponement to attempt reconciliation, and the plaintiff's request for a preliminary injunction was approved. It is now learned that during the postponement, Jiang Yang and others, through their attorneys, submitted a statement refuting the plaintiff's claims that she was Jiang Xingjie's concubine and regarding the amount of the estate. They stated that she was Xingjie's second wife, and Jiang Xingjie's will repeatedly referred to "wife Yang," as did the obituary, which referred to "Retiree" (Jiang Xingjie) in his self-description at age 50 in 1918 as "Yang succeeding in managing the household." The plaintiff's claim that she was not a spouse was unreasonable. As for the plaintiff's claim that Xingjie's estate was three million, the ten-odd mu of land on Jing'an Temple Road, Baker Road, and Parker Road, and the ten-odd mu of land on Yokohoma Bridge, have never been owned by the Jiang family. The plaintiff should bear the burden of proof. Furthermore, the will clearly stated that debts owed amounted to over 470,000, totaling over 600,000 with interest, all secured by property. This was merely the plaintiff's empty claim. Moreover, the plaintiff included in the estate a portion that Jiang Xingjie had given to others before his death and her own personal property, which was inappropriate. Therefore, if division was necessary, the estate should be cleared to thoroughly resolve the matter. It was requested that the lawsuit be suspended until Jiang Xingjie's estate had been cleared of debts, and that one-tenth of the remaining balance be distributed to the plaintiff, dismissing the plaintiff's lawsuit. An appeal was also filed with the Second Branch of the High Court against the preliminary injunction issued by the First Special Court. Yesterday morning, Judge Peng Shi continued the hearing in Civil Chamber Four. The attorneys for the plaintiff and defendant, He Shiming, Wang Fuchang, and Jiang Yiping, stated that both parties had reached an agreement on principles outside of court. The terms were that each side would nominate one or two representatives to form an estate clearing committee to handle the company clearing and analysis according to the following methods: (1) Determine the types and items of Jiang Xingjie's estate. (2) Determine Jiang Xingjie's debts before his death and the debts belonging to the estate, their items, amounts, and payment schedule. (3) Jiang Yang's personal property shall not be included in the estate. The standards are as follows: (A) Property originally registered under Jiang Yang's personal name before the start of inheritance and items for personal use should be considered her personal property. (B) Property transferred to Jiang Yang's name after the start of inheritance should be considered Jiang Xingjie's estate. (4) The method of estate division and the shares to be received by each person should be discussed and consulted with reference to how Xingjie's estate was handled. A contract has been established and should be recorded in the minutes, and the lawsuit should be suspended. Judge Peng approved this and announced that the lawsuit should be suspended.

Nine People Detained from Each Side

Wu Wenhai Accused of Selling a Young Woman 113

Improper Jurisdiction; Lawsuit Should Be Filed with the First Special Court

Zhu Qufeng, a 59-year-old man from Nantong currently residing at the Nanshi Security and Nursing Home, has a biological daughter named Yuqing, who is 16 years old this year. She had been betrothed and sent to her future husband's family as a child bride, but the daughter was unhappy, and the marriage was dissolved, requiring Zhu to return the betrothal gifts. Unable to raise the funds, Zhu borrowed money from Wu Wenhai, a man from Wuxi residing at No. 9 Chunde Lane, Lanweiai Road, French Concession, to cover the debt. After taking his daughter back, he placed her in Wu's home as a maid. Zhu recently learned that his daughter Yuqing had been sold by Wu Wenhai to the Jin family residence of Jin Yuntang in Dujia Lane, Nanhui, Pudong, as a daughter-in-law, and had already been married. Zhu reported the matter to the Songshan Road police station on April 13, requesting an investigation. Zhu claimed that his daughter had been taken out by Zhu from a stove shop at the intersection of Gordon Road and Avenue Road. The police station did not accept the case, as the crime scene was not in the French Concession. Recently, Zhu hired a lawyer to file a self-accusation of obstructing public morals against Wu Wenhai with the Criminal Division of the Second Special Court, requesting a trial. According to the accusation, the court, yesterday, held a hearing presided over by Judge Zhang Chaozuo. The accuser Zhu Qufeng arrived with his lawyer, but the defendant Wu Wenhai did not appear. According to the accuser, his daughter, Yuqing, who is 16 years old this year, was born on May 13, 1921, the Year of the Rooster. She had been betrothed to the tiger stove shop at the intersection of Gordon Road and Avenue Road as a child bride. On July 12 of last year, she was taken out by Wu Wenhai's daughter, Wu Yu, and hidden at No. 20 Hengfeng Lane, Bazilu. After being found by the groom's family, they rejected the girl, and I paid the silver to take my daughter back and placed her in Wu's home as a helper. Unexpectedly, the defendant and his daughter colluded to sell my daughter to the Jin family in Pudong as a daughter-in-law. I request an investigation. The court reviewed the evidence and, considering that the crime scene provided by the accuser was in the Public Concession, ruled that the lawsuit should be filed with the First Special District Court. The court then ruled that the jurisdiction was improper.

Home of Chinese Head Constable Zhang Xinghai Robbed and Plundered 114

Losses Exceed 3,000 Yuan - Three Bandits Captured

Zhang Xinghai, a Chinese head constable at the Hongkou Police Station, originally from Beiping, has served the Municipal Council for over ten years. His home is located at No. 8 Longzhi Lane, Kangnaotuo Road, West Shanghai. On April 6 of this year, several bandits armed with weapons suddenly broke into his home, preventing anyone from making noise, and ransacked the house for over an hour. They stole silver dollars and banknotes worth 1,000 yuan, as well as jewelry and clothing worth 2,020 yuan, and fled with the stolen goods. Head Constable Zhang reported the incident to the police station for investigation. Recently, Chinese Detective Feng Baishun, Detective Yao Changmin, Xia Shikui, Wang Dianchen, and others from the Chengdu Road Police Station learned that the gang was hiding at No. 100 Feihong Road, Zhabei. They coordinated with police detectives from the Public Security Bureau and secretly went to the address, arresting the bandits Yang Benzhang from Anhui and his mistress Yang Tian. They found two handguns, three bullets, and 57.5 yuan in banknotes, one gold ring, and a pair of earrings in a rice bag. According to Yang's confession, they also arrested Ge Xueshan, an accomplice, at No. 126 Shunqing Lane, Dafeng Road, Zhabei. However, Ge was well-informed and fled over the rooftops upon seeing the detectives, escaping capture. Later, Li Desheng, an accomplice from Anhui, was arrested on Zhonghua Road and brought back to the police station separately. Yesterday morning, they were sent to Criminal Chamber Eight of the First Special Court. Police attorney Zhang Tianyin stated the case and said that the police investigation was not yet complete, so Ge Laoxiao, Chen Jintang, Xiaoyang and others went to rob him. At that time, Xiaoyang and I each held a pistol, and Li Desheng was on the lookout at the alley entrance. Afterward, I received 500 yuan, and Li received 90 yuan. Someone named Zhang works as a maid in a certain family in Longzhi Lane and is having an affair with a rickshaw puller. Later, after Yang's wife was dismissed, they discussed the robbery. Li Desheng had gone to Longzhi Lane three times beforehand to scout. Yang Tian is my mistress and has been in Shanghai for not long. She knows nothing about this case. Li Desheng's testimony was evasive, denying any participation in the robbery. Judge Huang Risheng, after reviewing the confessions, ordered that Yang and the other three be detained for seven days for further interrogation. Yang Tian's child, Yang Liukouzi, was temporarily sent to the Women and Children's Relief Association for care.

Indian Man Van Jifu Da Travels the World, Arrives in Shanghai 115

The Shanghai Times reported that Fan Jifu Da, an Indian man and graduate of the University of Mumbai, is 22 years old. He began his world tour two years ago and, two months ago, traveled through the Chinese mainland on a motorcycle, first to Nanchang, then to Hangzhou, Nanjing, and Suzhou. He arrived in Shanghai on Friday (the 12th). Mr. Fan stated that traveling through the Chinese mainland on a motorcycle is no longer a major difficulty. Although the roads vary in quality, none are excessively poor. Mr. Fan has given lectures in many places along the way, using this to raise travel expenses, and he relies heavily on Chinese people to translate for him. However, when speaking in English at the Rotary Club of Nanjing and other organizations, listeners did not need translation. His lectures are mostly about Indian affairs. Mr. Fan plans to go north to Pingjin, but his movements will largely depend on the development and changes in the political situation. If going north is unstable, he plans to visit Japan instead. Before arriving in the Far East, Mr. Fan had traveled to India and Ceylon, then to Australia, visiting Melbourne, where the World Scout Jamboree was being held. Mr. Fan, being a Boy Scout from Mumbai and having many years of involvement with the Indian Boy Scout movement, participated in the event. The centennial anniversary of the opening of Melbourne was also held at that time, and he was able to attend the grand occasion. Mr. Fan was bitten by a poisonous spider in Australia and was hospitalized for five months, which delayed his stay for a long time. Mr. Fan set out on his journey on May 20, 1934, and has traveled over 7,500 miles to date. He plans to stay in Shanghai for two weeks, then return to India via Japan, the United States, the United Kingdom, and the European continent. It is expected to take another two years to complete this 25,000-mile journey.

Hygiene Exhibition Also Held at the People's Education Center - Regular Training on Hygiene Knowledge for Public Places

The annual hygiene campaign, this year's (15th), has been jointly prepared by the Hygiene Bureau and the New Life Movement Promotion Association, along with various agencies and organizations, for the past month. It is now ready, and the scale is larger than before. It is scheduled to officially open tomorrow (the 15th) at the People's Education Center on Wenmiao Road and will last until the end of the month. The details are as follows:

Opening Ceremony - At 10:00 AM, the opening ceremony will be held in the lecture hall of the center. Honorary Vice Presidents Yang Hu, Pan Gongzhan, Wu Xingya, Cai Jinjun, Yu Hongjun, and Tong Xingbai, as well as President Li Ting'an and Vice President Shen Gao and Zhu Erden, will form the presidium to preside over everything. First, Mayor Wu will be invited to cut the ribbon for the exhibition and inspect it for a week. Then, the meeting will begin. The order is as follows: (1) Opening of the meeting, (2) Music (Public Security Bureau Band), (3) Singing of the Party Anthem, (4) Paying the highest respects to the Party, the national flag, and the portrait of Sun Yat-sen, (5) The chairman respectfully reads Sun Yat-sen's will, (6) Silence, (7) The president reports, (8) The chairman gives instructions, (9) Speech, (10) Singing of the hygiene song, (11) Music, (12) Photography, (13) Major cleanup, (14) Adjournment.

Conference Staff - (1) Presidium: Honorary President Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Honorary Vice Presidents Commander Yang Xiaotian, Director Pan Gongzhan, Director Wu Xingya, Director Cai Jinjun, Secretary-General Yu Hongjun, Committee Member Tong Xingbai, President Director Li Ting'an, Vice Presidents Director Zhu Erden, Section Chief Shen Gao. (2) Staff: Secretary-General Zhu Jiarang, Deputy Secretaries-General Wu Zhongyao, Zhang Shousong, Master of Ceremonies Yu Pu, Chief Receptionist Zhu Xiaochun, Receptionists Li Ziyang, Wu Gang, Ling Xitao, Zhou Guoshi, Lei Kenan, Lin Yannan, Cao Zhigong, Cao Changling, Yan Sen, Chief Disciplinarian Yuan Liangzou, Disciplinarians Du Hesheng, Yu Da, Xie Yanbo, Zhou Xuexiang, Yin Yong, Recorders Wu Zhongyao, Zhang Shousong.

Activity Schedule - After the opening ceremony tomorrow, around 11:00 AM, the cleaning and labor service work will begin. The area will first be the Ximen District. Approximately 1,000 people, including members of the Youth Service Corps, the Security Corps, police officers, security teams, and street sweepers, will gather on Wenmiao Road with brooms and cleaning supplies. After the major cleanup ceremony, they will immediately begin operations in their assigned areas, performing six service items: sweeping roads, cleaning walls, organizing lanes and alleys, guiding shops in fly control, and discouraging spitting. The conference venue will also have a central activity scheduled for each day. Tomorrow, the first day, will be Children's Clothing Hygiene Guidance Day, starting at 1:00 PM, hosted by the Hygiene Bureau.

Hygiene Exhibition - This year's hygiene exhibition is being held in a mat shed built on the open space of the People's Education Center. Exhibits are being displayed by the Ministry of Health, the Health Bureau, and the Public Concession Health Department, among others. The content and quantity are both very rich and excellent. They have now been arranged and will open tomorrow, closing at the end of the month, lasting about sixteen days. It is expected that the audience will be very enthusiastic, which will greatly benefit society.

Hygiene Promotion - The preparatory committee, in order to expand promotion, has not only posted colored slogans throughout the city and printed summer hygiene common sense propaganda, but has also invited Mayor Wu, Director Li, and Commander Yang to broadcast hygiene speeches on the municipal government's Fuyin Chinese and Western radio stations to broaden the promotion.

Hygiene Training - The conference promotion committee believes that public places such as restaurants and entertainment venues have a greater impact on the well-being of citizens if they do not pay attention to hygiene. Therefore, it is necessary to emphasize supervision of this type of business. The most fundamental method is to convene these shop owners and instill in them basic hygiene knowledge so that they know how to improve. Therefore, this year's hygiene campaign has a provision for hygiene knowledge training in public places. It is scheduled to start on the 16th. Shop owners of teahouses, restaurants, bathhouses, barbershops, hot water shops, inns, apartments, tofu shops, butcher shops, vegetable markets, and entertainment venues must personally or send a representative to the Shanghai South, Shanghai North, Gaoqiao, Wusong, and Jiangwan Five Hygiene Offices to register and await training. It is reported that the Social Affairs and Public Security Bureaus have also forwarded notices to various industries, preparing them to receive training.

Invitation to All Sectors - Municipal Health Bureau Director Li Ting'an, in order to express his gratitude for the assistance from all parties in organizing this hygiene campaign and to arouse the attention of all sectors, specially sent letters to the heads of various agencies and leaders of all sectors in this city yesterday, inviting them to come to the venue for guidance.

昨日天氣驟熱 124

Yesterday's Weather Suddenly Turned Hot

Highest Temperature 88.7 Degrees

Cold Drink Stalls Triple Their Profits

The weather in the city was extremely hot yesterday, especially at noon. The highest temperature was 88.7 degrees, recorded between 1:30 PM and 1:00 PM. The lowest temperature was 65.7 degrees. During the same period last year, the highest temperature was 85 degrees and the lowest was 62.6 degrees. Yesterday was the hottest day in the past six months of this year. Pedestrians on the road were wearing very light clothing, but it was still too hot. Because it was the first time this year that it suddenly turned so hot, people were not used to the scorching sun. Cold drink stalls on the roadside, selling items such as shaved ice and ice cream, tripled their profits.

Changes to Hankou Road One-Way Traffic Starting on the 15th

8:00 AM to 9:00 AM and 1:00 PM to 2:00 PM Designated as Times for Eastbound Traffic, 12:00 PM to 1:00 PM Westbound

The Public Concession Municipal Council has decided to change the one-way traffic regulations for Hankou Road starting from the 15th of this month. The General Manager Zhong Si issued Public Notice No. 4715, which states:

Notice is hereby given that the one-way traffic rules on Hankou Road have been amended, abolishing the existing restrictions from 4:30 PM to 5:30 PM. Effective from June 15, 1936, Article 40 (E) of the Traffic Regulations shall be amended as follows: Except on Sundays and public holidays, all vehicles, during the following times, shall only be allowed one-way traffic on the section of Hankou Road between Henan Road and Xizang Road, but rickshaws are not included:

Eastbound: 8:00 AM to 9:00 AM, 1:00 PM to 2:00 PM

Westbound: 12:00 PM to 1:00 PM

Hereby announced for public knowledge.

平安　船塢「客松」被冲經過 130

Details of Ping An Dock's "Caisson" Being Washed Away

Not Due to Years of Disrepair, But Due to High Tide

The Ping An Dock, belonging to the Gongmao Machinery Shipbuilding Plant, is located at the mouth of Bailianjing, Pudong. The location is ideal, and it is the only commercial dock. It has been in operation for forty years, starting in the 14th year of the Guangxu reign of the Qing Dynasty, and was operated by the late merchant Zheng Liangyu. The dock is 260 feet long, 8 feet wide, and 12 feet deep, which is very suitable for the repair of general ships. The dock fees are low, which is very popular with the shipping industry. After minor repairs this year, the dock work is even busier. The dock's caisson has been used frequently, and for convenience, it was originally planned to add safety equipment to ensure stability. The management carefully considered the matter and consulted shipbuilding experts to ensure that it would meet the needs. It was in the process of estimating the labor and materials for construction when, on the morning of the 10th of this month, it was impacted by a high tide, causing an irresistible accident. The caisson itself is completely a floating cuboid. If the dock has no water, due to the imbalance of water pressure, if the ballast at the bottom is lacking, there is a risk of it being washed away. The dock has always had experience in managing the dock and guiding ships in and out. This Huangpu high tide has been happening for three days. On the afternoon of the 9th, it was also around 13 feet. The sudden impact at 2:00 AM on the 10th was unexpected. The Minsheng Industrial Company's Min Duo ship, which was being repaired in the dock, was not yet completed and suffered the disaster. Fortunately, the loss was not great. Manager Zheng and Manager Zhang of the Minsheng Company have a good relationship with the factory's management and expressed sympathy for the dock's accident. The Gongmao Shipbuilding Plant will completely repair the damaged parts of the Min Duo ship, which shows their business integrity and is very admirable. The dock has been working hard for two days to reorganize and has already completed the work. The planned repair work has also been renewed. From now on, it will be more convenient for ships to enter the dock for repair and inspection. It is reported that the factory will revise the new dock fee collection rate to help alleviate the shipping industry's recession.

西顏料業昨會議緝私 134

Western Paint Industry Held Meeting Yesterday to Combat Smuggling

The Western Paint Industry Association believes that smuggling has recently become rampant. In order to assist the authorities in combating smuggling, it should engage in inspection work. At the same time, in order to facilitate sales, the Association will be responsible for proving and reporting shipments of paints packaged into smaller containers. The Association held its 18th Executive Supervisory Meeting yesterday. Committee members Ma Shangjie, Xi Jinggeng, Wang Zuolin, Wang Peng, Li Shuyan, and others, totaling more than ten people, attended. Ma Shangjie presided over the meeting and submitted the following proposals: (A) Discuss the letters from Gonghe Lai, Tailai, and Yongfeng Chang, requesting a solution to the problem that the customs does not allow the reporting of "paints in smaller containers," hindering business. Resolution: This case should be referred to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to be forwarded to the Ministry of Finance, ordering all customs offices that for the industry to ship smaller container paint, attach the association’s certification and paste the association's inspection certificate with the goods to effectively prove that it is permitted to be reported as usual to facilitate business. The drafting was revised and sent. (B) Discuss the establishment of a smuggling reporting committee to implement inspection work and assist the government in combating smuggling. Resolution: A smuggling reporting committee should be established. All members of the Executive Committee will serve concurrently as members to handle inspection and smuggling suppression matters. Passed. (C) It was decided that the date of the Association's general meeting of members would be at 1:00 PM on June 25th at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce for re-election according to law. Passed. (The rest omitted.) Adjourned.

Publishing Industry 140

Reissue of the Second Volume of the Humorous Cartoon "Ox-Nose" Huang Yao's "Ox-Nose" has long been the first humorous cartoon character in China that is welcomed by everyone. Its style is unique, and it uses extremely simple lines to construct extremely vivid and lively expressions and postures. The drawing method of Ox-Nose is used to organize the cartoons, without adding a single point or stroke, or borrowing text or background as a foil. Naturally, it expresses extremely vivid and humorous content with deep satirical meaning, ridiculing people from all walks of life. It needs to be deeply speculated and distinguished, and its humor is timeless. Old and young alike hold a copy in their hands and never tire of reading it. Therefore, major newspapers and magazines in the north and south are vying to invite special publications and respond with welcome. Letter 143

To the Editor, I have just read in today's newspaper a news item about the opening of the Xuzhou Highway, which stated that it was built by the "Chinese and Foreign Relief Association." Please note that the name of our association is the "China Chinese and Foreign Relief and Disaster Relief Association," abbreviated as the "Chinese and Foreign Relief Association." It is a group registered with the Ministry of Interior and has obtained legal person status. In order to provide relief to the disaster victims in northern Jiangsu, the Subei Yellow Disaster Relief and Industrial Reconstruction Office was established in February of this year to carry out the Xuhai Second Release Road Project. The Xufang project plans to build five roads, namely Tongpei, Tongdang, Tongshui, Tongsuyi, and Tongxiao, with a total length of 150 li, and 10 li of ring road. The Haifang road construction starts from Xiangshuikou to Banpu, and then turns northwest to Xinpu, with a total length of 130 li. It has not yet been completed. The roads built in Xuzhou have been completed last week. After the opening ceremony is held on the 12th of this month, the Jiangsu Provincial Government and the Tong District Commissioner's Office will accept the acceptance and open it to traffic. The newspaper mistakenly called it the "Chinese and Foreign Relief Association," which is neither the abbreviation used by our association, nor does it easily raise suspicions from the outside world, and it does not affect the credibility of our association with donors. Accordingly, we send a special letter to declare this, hoping to check and correct it. Sincerely, The China Chinese and Foreign Relief and Disaster Relief Association Shanghai Office, 25, 6, 13,

A General Review of the Athletics Selection 148

— Huaiqing

Since the announcement of the candidates for the World Games athletics team, the criticism from the outside world has been truly "uproarious" and a spectacular sight. The controversy over the basketball team has long passed; the so-called amateur event of the football team is also called the "aftermath"; and now the error in the athletics selection is becoming more and more widespread. It has become the "autumn of troubles" in the domestic sports world for the sake of attending the World Games! "Those who speak are sincere, those who listen are indifferent", how can it be the attitude that the parties concerned should have?

The error in the athletics selection has become an undeniable fact. The resolution of the National Sports Association Board of Directors has become nothing more than "a piece of paper". The selection method and standards have completely overturned this resolution. With the rashness of a few people, and the "people" issue, without overall planning, it has led to the current great mistake. Now I want to analyze it item by item based on the facts. But I must state that I express my respect for the elected athletes and have no discrimination against them; I do not feel injustice for the unsuccessful athletes, and I do not particularly promote them; I have no evil intentions in aiming at the authorities; I am completely making a whole review based on the situation unfolding before us.

(One)

According to the legal publication of the National Sports Association - "Sports Quarterly" Volume 2, Issue 1: "Item 4 of the Second Meeting Record of the Third Board of Directors on January 27, 25: Appoint and retroactively recognize the list of selection committee members for various sports participating in the World Games, and set the selection principles as follows: good character, excellent performance, younger age and hope for training. Athletics and swimming selection committee members: John Ma (convener), Rong Qizhao, Zhou Jiaqi, ... Also set the pre-selection performance standards for participation."

There are three athletics and swimming selection committee members. Rong Qizhao has led the Chinese football team abroad, and Zhou Jiaqi has also gone abroad earlier to meet the football team fighting in Java and then go to Germany to arrange everything. Only John Ma is still in the country and is responsible for the athletics selection and training. After Rong and Zhou went abroad, no announcement of the personnel acting for the athletics selection committee was seen. So, is this selection matter entirely presided over by Mr. Ma alone? Or jointly responsible by other officials of the National Sports Association? Why not announce it in advance?

(Two)

According to the National Sports Association's same issue of the Sports Quarterly: "Table of Pre-Selection Athletics Performance Standards for Participating in the World Games", a comparison is made with the pre-selection performance as follows:

(Note: ×The first place in the 200-meter race was British Bowan, with a score of 22.7 seconds, dropping Liu by 56 meters. At that time, because Liu was the second place and there was no definite time to announce. According to Jiang Xiangqing's "Criticism of Athletics Selection" article in the 11th Times News, it was 23.4 seconds)

The above table does not have the pre-selection standards for the ten-item event and the marathon. That is, there was no by-election in the order of the pre-selection day. Then, there is no doubt that these two items are scheduled not to send athletes. Until the day of confrontation, suddenly the radio broadcasted the test of the ten-item event; without announcing it and without explaining it, what reason can be used to say that sending athletes for the ten-item event is legitimate? What reason can be used to say that sending marathon athletes is not illegal? Moreover, among the currently announced athletes, whether their scores have met the standard scores, participating in the pre-selection, they still have to meet the standard scores, then the performance standard for selecting World Games athletes must at least reach the pre-selection standard, and it is ironclad that it should surpass this pre-selection standard.

There is also a table of pre-selection standard scores for participation, and the standards set are as follows:

There are pre-selection standard scores for women, and a total of nine people were reported to participate in the women's pre-selection. Except for Li Sen, the others did not participate. They gave up on their own. Why did Mr. John Ma, the convener of the athletics selection committee, give a speech to the newspaper reporters, saying that "As for women's sports, I have always advocated it very much, but in view of the performance and physiological protection, participating in the World Games seems too early." (This talk can be found in Shanghai newspapers on June 6) Since the women's pre-selection standards have been set, this is of course wanting to send female athletes; and why did Mr. Ma say "Participating in the World Games seems too early"? Therefore, the absence of the female athletes who signed up for the pre-selection can be said to be all because of Mr. Ma's words. However, since women's participation in the World Games is too early, why send a female athlete to participate? How is this explained?

(Three)

Since the pre-selection performance standards and selection principles have been announced, of course, they must be followed according to the announced intention. The number of people selected is twelve. Since the end of the training class in Beiping and after the end, Mr. John Ma and Liu Changchun (captain of the training class) have repeatedly stated that they want to increase the number of people selected to sixteen. When Liu arrived in Shanghai, he also stated to the newspaper reporters. There was nothing wrong with increasing the number to sixteen, but the National Sports Association did not formally announce it. Until the announcement of the selected candidates, it did increase to sixteen. Moreover, there are representatives sent for the programs that are not in the pre-selection order, and those who did not meet the pre-selection standard scores were also selected, and several people with pre-selection standard scores were also not selected; this inconsistency between words and deeds fundamentally overturned the selection standards, which is contrary to the principle of "administration." Could it be that the leaders of the national sports world can be so negligent about such a big thing?

(Four)

Now I want to talk about the issue of Zhang Lingjia, the representative of the ten-item event. After this issue was pointed out, Mr. John Ma immediately gave an explanation. He said: "... Zhang Lingjia, the representative of the ten-item event, is considered to be improperly selected by the outside world. I don't know that Mr. Zhang's spirit of hard work is very good, and he has a good understanding of psychology. Our country is participating in the World Games this time for observation purposes, and participating in ten items will benefit more. And Mr. Zhang has decided to serve the sports world after returning to China..." We do not object to sending representatives for the ten-item event, but why not announce it in advance to give others the same opportunity? Moreover, does Mr. Zhang's performance meet the principle of "excellent performance"? Mr. Zhang's "spirit of hard work is very good... After returning to China, he has decided to serve the sports world." In order to improve performance, who does not have this spirit of hard work? Who can say that he has decided not to serve the sports world after returning to China? This is very illogical. Moreover, Mr. Zhang's sports era has passed. He is neither "younger in age" nor "excellent in performance". According to Dong Yinchu's "Question" Item 3 "Zhang Lingjia, a ten-item athlete, is listed as an assistant teacher in the Department of Physical Education on the Tsinghua University list. Does this conflict with the amateur qualifications?" (See the 17th Times News) Since Mr. Dong discovered that Zhang was an assistant teacher in the Department of Physical Education on the Tsinghua University list, it is presumably not a fabricated slander. If so, he is no longer an amateur athlete. Then the so-called "spirit of hard work" and "After returning to China, he has decided to serve the sports world" and "Participating in ten items will benefit more" have logical fallacies, which is very obvious. The matter concerns the national face and must not be played with negligence. Given this, all the debates about Zhang Lingjia, the athlete of the ten-item event, should be completely overturned, and Mr. Zhang's right to represent should be revoked immediately. The amateur style of football has been enough, and we do not want athletics to have such a shameful thing again. Moreover, John Ma also talked about the issue of Li Huitang. He said: "The Li Huitang incident concerns the national face, and it is advocated to investigate it strictly"; we should ask Mr. Ma to lead by example and "strictly investigate" Zhang Lingjia's qualifications first.

(Five)

As Mr. Ma said, "Mr. Zhang's spirit of hard work is very good" and "After returning to China, he has decided to serve the sports world", I should add one more sentence "Mr. Zhang's character is good". Mr. Zhang has a long sports life and indeed has the above-mentioned virtues. He can indeed make considerable contributions in the sports world; this time, our country should definitely give him an opportunity to participate in the World Games; but he should not be illegally selected as a representative for the ten-item event. Why not send him to the inspection team?

We hope that the sixteen athletes should be strictly reviewed, and at least those who meet the pre-selection standard scores are qualified to represent China to participate in the World Games. If the funding is sufficient, it is possible to organize a "sightseeing tour" for all the lagging athletes who are not far from the pre-selection standard scores and who meet the three principles of selection, and accompany them to Germany for sightseeing, which can also gain some technical and construction knowledge. Or give those who have deeper qualifications and seem unable to continue exercising, such as Liu Changchun, Zhang Lingjia, and Hao Chunde, etc., and do not want them to continue exercising in the future. Give them the title of "coach" with a clear conscience and give them the opportunity to participate in the World Games, hoping that they will honestly be instructors after returning to China.

It is not a smart way to blame the error in selection; it is not bright to advocate for a certain unsuccessful athlete; the authorities' persistence and failure to empathize, and failure to plan good policies, is not an attitude that the highest sports authorities and leaders in the country should have; I hope to seek an irresistible compromise based on the above-mentioned fifth point. (Night of June 12)

Kangdi Tennis Department Initiates Open Tournament 153

Given the absence of an open tennis championship organized by Chinese players in Shanghai, the Kangdi Sports Association recently convened a competition committee, deciding to hold the Kangdi Open Men's Singles and Doubles Tennis Championships. The singles competition is scheduled to begin on July 11th, with the finals on the 25th. The doubles competition is scheduled to begin on July 18th, with the finals on the 26th. The entry fee is three yuan for singles and five yuan for doubles. The association will provide all balls (though the type of ball has not yet been decided). Except for the semi-finals and finals, which will be best-of-five sets, all other rounds will be best-of-three sets. To increase the competition's appeal, invitations will be extended to tennis clubs (including foreign clubs) and top players from various schools in Shanghai. Registration is open from today onwards at the Kangdi Sports Association on Kangdi Road and the Huadong Sporting Goods Company on Jing'an Temple Road. It is hoped that all famous players in Shanghai will actively participate.

Committee Members Present: Pan Gongzhan, Lei Zhen (substituting for Xue), Wu Yan Yin, Chen Heqin, Xue Tianhan, Fan Shou Zang, (substituting for Xue), Gu Shusen, (substituting for Wu), Hu Shuyi, Chen Nianzhong, (substituting for Yang Junqin), Yang Junquan, Gao Yinzhu, Wu Shizhong, Luo Yunyan, Yu Ziyi, Gao Junshan, Zhu Zhanggeng, etc. Chairman: Pan Gongzhan; Recorder: Xue Tianhan.

Discussion of Proposals: The proposal to establish the organizational regulations for the National Child Welfare Enterprise Association was approved, with revisions to the original regulations. The association will submit these regulations to the Ministry of Interior and Education for submission to the Executive Yuan for approval. Regarding the selection of committee members in Article 2, the Central Propaganda Committee should recommend one person, and preference should be given to those already working in children's welfare organizations. Regarding the association's funding, the Standing Committee will first prepare a budget, which the association will then submit to the Ministry of Interior and Education for submission to the Executive Yuan for approval. The proposal to establish the organizational charter for the preparatory committee for the National Children's Hygiene Exhibition and the Year of the Child Closing Celebration was approved, with revisions to the original charter. The decision to approve the budget for the National Children's Hygiene Exhibition was made. The Standing Committee will approve the budget, but an item for sanitary materials, which was missing from the original budget, should be added appropriately. The proposal on how to hold the Year of the Child Closing Ceremony was approved. The Standing Committee will be requested to formulate measures for the Year of the Child Closing Ceremony, which the association will forward to the Year of the Child Implementation Committees in various regions for implementation. The proposal on whether to hold a summer children's health camp this year was approved. Committee Member Song Zhangyang will be asked to formulate a plan for organizing the summer children's health camp, referring to the measures taken last year, and send it to the Standing Committee for review. The association will then distribute it to the Year of the Child Implementation Committees in various provinces and cities for compliance. The suggestion to provide relief to poor children was approved. This suggestion should be handled by the Central Child Welfare Enterprise Association after its organization is established. The request to forward a proposal to the Executive Yuan, ordering the Ministry of Transportation and the Ministry of Railways to revise the half-price fare policy for children traveling by boat and train, was approved. The association will formulate measures to provide preferential treatment for children (individuals or groups) traveling by boat and train and submit them to the Ministry of Interior and Education for submission to the Executive Yuan, ordering the Ministry of Transportation and the Ministry of Railways to improve these measures. For the sake of the health and safety of elementary school children, the proposal to request the association to submit a request to the Ministry of Education, ordering all elementary schools in the country to pay attention to five practical issues in children's education, was approved in principle. The association will submit a request to the Ministry of Education, ordering all elementary schools in the country to pay attention to these issues. The proposal on which proposals the association should submit to the Second Municipal Child Welfare Congress was approved. The Standing Committee will decide on these proposals. If any committee members have proposals, they should submit them to the Standing Committee for approval by the end of this month. The proposal on how to promote the Central Children's Education Museum was approved. The association will formulate an organizational plan for the Central Children's Education Museum at the next general assembly and transfer it to the Central Child Welfare Enterprise Association for handling.
